 47→\t// DebounceAfter is the delay added to events to wait\n    48→\t// after a registry/config event for debouncing.\n    49→\t// This will delay the push by at least this interval, plus\n    50→\t// the time getting subsequent events. If no change is\n    51→\t// detected the push will happen, otherwise we'll keep\n    52→\t// delaying until things settle.\n    53→\tDebounceAfter time.Duration\n    54→\n    55→\t// debounceMax is the maximum time to wait for events\n    56→\t// while debouncing. If events keep\n    57→\t// showing up with no break for this time, we'll trigger a push.\n    58→\tdebounceMax time.Duration\n    59→\n    60→\t// enableEDSDebounce indicates whether EDS pushes should be debounced.\n    61→\tenableEDSDebounce bool\n    62→}\n    63→\n    64→// DiscoveryServer is Pilot's gRPC implementation for Envoy's xds APIs\n    65→type DiscoveryServer struct {\n    66→\t// Env is the model environment.\n    67→\tEnv *model.Environment\n    68→\n    69→\t// Generators allow customizing the generated config, based on the client metadata.\n    70→\t// Key is the generator type - will match the Generator metadata to set the per-connection\n    71→\t// default generator, or the combination of Generator metadata and TypeUrl to select a\n    72→\t// different generator for a type.\n    73→\t// Normal istio clients use the default generator - will not be impacted by this.\n    74→\tGenerators map[string]model.XdsResourceGenerator\n    75→\n    76→\t// ProxyNeedsPush is a function that determines whether a push can be completely skipped. 136→\n   137→\tkrtDebugger *krt.DebugHandler\n   138→}\n   139→\n   140→// NewDiscoveryServer creates DiscoveryServer that sources data from Pilot's internal mesh data structures\n   141→func 213→\n   214→func (s *DiscoveryServer) Start(stopCh <-chan struct{}) {\n   215→\tgo s.WorkloadEntryController.Run(stopCh)\n   216→\tgo s.handleUpdates(stopCh)\n   217→\tgo *DiscoveryServer) periodicRefreshMetrics(stopCh <-chan struct{}) {\n   224→\tticker := time.NewTicker(periodicRefreshMetrics)\n   225→\tdefer ticker.Stop()\n   226→\tfor {\n   227→\t\tselect {\n   228→\t\tcase <-ticker.C:\n   229→\t\t\tpush := s.globalPushContext()\n   230→\t\t\tmodel.LastPushMutex.Lock()\n   231→\t\t\tif model.LastPushStatus != push {\n   232→\t\t\t\tmodel.LastPushStatus = push\n   233→\t\t\t\tpush.UpdateMetrics()\n   234→\t\t\t\tout, _ := model.LastPushStatus.StatusJSON()\n   235→\t\t\t\tif string(out) != \"{}\" {\n   236→\t\t\t\t\tlog.Infof(\"Push Status: %s\", string(out))\n   237→\t\t\t\t}\n   238→\t\t\t}\n   239→\t\t\tmodel.LastPushMutex.Unlock()\n   240→\t\tcase <-stopCh:\n   241→\t\t\treturn\n   242→\t\t}\n   243→\t}\n   244→}\n   245→\n   246→// dropCacheForRequest clears the cache in response to a push request\n   247→func (s *DiscoveryServer) dropCacheForRequest(req *model.PushRequest) {\n   248→\t// If we don't know what updated, cannot safely cache. Clear the whole cache\n   249→\tif req.Forced {\n   250→\t\ts.Cache.ClearAll()\n   251→\t} else {\n   252→\t\t// Otherwise, just clear the updated configs\n   253→\t\ts.Cache.Clear(req.ConfigsUpdated)\n   254→\t}\n   255→}\n   256→\n   257→// Push is called to push changes on config updates using ADS.\n   258→func (s *DiscoveryServer) Push(req *model.PushRequest) {\n   259→\tif !req.Full {\n   260→\t\treq.Push = s.globalPushContext()\n   261→\t\ts.dropCacheForRequest(req)\n   262→\t\ts.AdsPushAll(req)\n   263→\t\treturn\n   264→\t}\n   265→\t// Reset the status during the push.\n   266→\toldPushContext := s.globalPushContext()\n   267→\tif oldPushContext != nil {\n   268→\t\toldPushContext.OnConfigChange()\n   269→\t\t// Push the previous push Envoy metrics.\n   270→\t\tenvoyfilter.RecordMetrics()\n   271→\t}\n   272→\t// PushContext is reset after a config change. Previous status is\n   273→\t// saved.\n   274→\tt0 := time.Now()\n   275→\tversionLocal := s.NextVersion()\n   276→\tpush := s.initPushContext(req, oldPushContext, versionLocal)\n   277→\tinitContextTime := time.Since(t0)\n   278→\tlog.Debugf(\"InitContext %v for push took %s\", versionLocal, initContextTime)\n   279→\tpushContextInitTime.Record(initContextTime.Seconds())\n   280→\n   281→\treq.Push = push\n   282→\ts.AdsPushAll(req)\n   283→}\n   284→\n   285→func nonce(noncePrefix string) string {\n   286→\treturn noncePrefix + uuid.New().String()\n   287→}\n   288→\n   289→// Returns the global push context. This should be used with caution; generally the proxy-specific\n   290→// PushContext should be used to get the current state in the context of a single proxy. This should\n   291→// only be used for \"global\" lookups, such as initiating a new push to all proxies.\n   292→func (s *DiscoveryServer) globalPushContext() *model.PushContext {\n   293→\treturn s.Env.PushContext()\n   294→}\n   295→\n   296→var fullPushLog = istiolog.RegisterScope(\"fullpush\", \"logs details about why Istio is triggering a full push\")\n   297→\n   298→// ConfigUpdate implements ConfigUpdater interface, used to request pushes.\n   299→func (s *DiscoveryServer) ConfigUpdate(req *model.PushRequest) {\n   300→\tif features.EnableUnsafeAssertions {\n   301→\t\tif model.HasConfigsOfKind(req.ConfigsUpdated, kind.Service) {\n   302→\t\t\tpanic(\"assertion failed kind.Service can not be set in ConfigKey\")\n   303→\t\t}\n   304→\t}\n   305→\tif model.HasConfigsOfKind(req.ConfigsUpdated, kind.Address) {\n   306→\t\t// This is a bit like clearing EDS cache on EndpointShard update. Because Address\n   307→\t\t// types are fetched dynamically, they are not part of the same protections, so we need to clear\n   308→\t\t// the cache.\n   309→\t\ts.Cache.ClearAll()\n   310→\t}\n   311→\tinboundConfigUpdates.Increment()\n   312→\ts.InboundUpdates.Inc()\n   313→\tif req.Full && fullPushLog.DebugEnabled() {\n   314→\t\tconfigs := slices.Sort(slices.Map(req.ConfigsUpdated.UnsortedList(), model.ConfigKey.String))\n   315→\t\treasons := maps.Keys(req.Reason)\n   316→\t\tfullPushLog.Debugf(\"full push triggered configs=%v reasons=%v\", configs, reasons)\n   317→\t}\n   318→\ts.pushChannel <- req\n   319→}\n   320→\n   321→// Debouncing and push request happens in a separate thread, it uses locks\n   322→// and we want to avoid complications, ConfigUpdate may already hold other locks.\n   323→// handleUpdates processes events from pushChannel\n   324→// It ensures that at minimum minQuiet time has elapsed since the last event before processing it.\n   325→// It also ensures that at most maxDelay is elapsed between receiving an event and processing it.\n   326→func (s *DiscoveryServer) handleUpdates(stopCh <-chan struct{}) {\n   327→\tdebounce(s.pushChannel, stopCh, s.DebounceOptions, s.Push, s.CommittedUpdates)\n   328→}\n   329→\n   330→// The debounce helper function is implemented to enable mocking\n   331→func debounce(ch chan *model.PushRequest, stopCh <-chan struct{}, opts DebounceOptions, pushFn func(req *model.PushRequest), updateSent *atomic.Int64) {\n   332→\tvar timeChan <-chan time.Time\n   333→\tvar startDebounce time.Time\n   334→\tvar lastConfigUpdateTime time.Time\n   335→\n   336→\tpushCounter := 0\n   337→\tdebouncedEvents := 0\n   338→\n   339→\t// Keeps track of the push requests. If updates are debounce they will be merged.\n   340→\tvar req *model.PushRequest\n   341→\n   342→\tfree := true\n   343→\tfreeCh := make(chan struct{}, 1)\n   344→\n   345→\tpush := func(req *model.PushRequest, debouncedEvents int, startDebounce time.Time) {\n   346→\t\tpushFn(req)\n   347→\t\tupdateSent.Add(int64(debouncedEvents))\n   348→\t\tdebounceTime.Record(time.Since(startDebounce).Seconds())\n   349→\t\tfreeCh <- struct{}{}\n   350→\t}\n   351→\n   352→\tpushWorker := func() {\n   353→\t\teventDelay := time.Since(startDebounce)\n   354→\t\tquietTime := time.Since(lastConfigUpdateTime)\n   355→\t\t// it has been too long or quiet enough\n   356→\t\tif eventDelay >= opts.debounceMax || quietTime >= opts.DebounceAfter {\n   357→\t\t\tif req != nil {\n   358→\t\t\t\tpushCounter++\n   359→\t\t\t\tif req.ConfigsUpdated == nil {\n   360→\t\t\t\t\tlog.Infof(\"Push debounce stable[%d] %d for reason %s: %v since last change, %v since last push, full=%v\",\n   361→\t\t\t\t\t\tpushCounter, debouncedEvents, reasonsUpdated(req),\n   362→\t\t\t\t\t\tquietTime, eventDelay, req.Full)\n   363→\t\t\t\t} else {\n   364→\t\t\t\t\tlog.Infof(\"Push debounce stable[%d] %d for config %s: %v since last change, %v since last push, full=%v\",\n   365→\t\t\t\t\t\tpushCounter, debouncedEvents, configsUpdated(req),\n   366→\t\t\t\t\t\tquietTime, eventDelay, req.Full)\n   367→\t\t\t\t}\n   368→\t\t\t\tfree = false\n   369→\t\t\t\tgo push(req, debouncedEvents, startDebounce)\n   370→\t\t\t\treq = nil\n   371→\t\t\t\tdebouncedEvents = 0\n   372→\t\t\t}\n   373→\t\t} else {\n   374→\t\t\ttimeChan = time.After(opts.DebounceAfter - quietTime)\n   375→\t\t}\n   376→\t}\n   377→\n   378→\tfor {\n   379→\t\tselect {\n   380→\t\tcase <-freeCh:\n   381→\t\t\tfree = true\n   382→\t\t\tpushWorker()\n   383→\t\tcase r := <-ch:\n   384→\t\t\t// If reason is not set, record it as an unknown reason\n   385→\t\t\tif len(r.Reason) == 0 {\n   386→\t\t\t\tr.Reason = model.NewReasonStats(model.UnknownTrigger)\n   387→\t\t\t}\n   388→\t\t\tif !opts.enableEDSDebounce && !r.Full {\n   389→\t\t\t\t// trigger push now, just for EDS\n   390→\t\t\t\tgo func(req *model.PushRequest) {\n   391→\t\t\t\t\tpushFn(req)\n   392→\t\t\t\t\tupdateSent.Inc()\n   393→\t\t\t\t}(r)\n   394→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   395→\t\t\t}\n   396→\n   397→\t\t\tlastConfigUpdateTime = time.Now()\n   398→\t\t\tif debouncedEvents == 0 {\n   399→\t\t\t\ttimeChan = time.After(opts.DebounceAfter)\n   400→\t\t\t\tstartDebounce = lastConfigUpdateTime\n   401→\t\t\t}\n   402→\t\t\tdebouncedEvents++\n   403→\n   404→\t\t\treq = req.Merge(r)\n   405→\t\tcase <-timeChan:\n   406→\t\t\tif free {\n   407→\t\t\t\tpushWorker()\n   408→\t\t\t}\n   409→\t\tcase <-stopCh:\n   410→\t\t\treturn\n   411→\t\t}\n   412→\t}\n   413→}\n   414→\n   415→func configsUpdated(req *model.PushRequest) string {\n   416→\tconfigs := \"\"\n   417→\tfor key := range req.ConfigsUpdated {\n   418→\t\tconfigs += key.String()\n   419→\t\tbreak\n   420→\t}\n   421→\tif len(req.ConfigsUpdated) > 1 {\n   422→\t\tmore := \" and \" + strconv.Itoa(len(req.ConfigsUpdated)-1) + \" more configs\"\n   423→\t\tconfigs += more\n   424→\t}\n   425→\treturn configs\n   426→}\n   427→\n   428→func reasonsUpdated(req *model.PushRequest) string {\n   429→\tvar (\n   430→\t\treason0, reason1            model.TriggerReason\n   431→\t\treason0Cnt, reason1Cnt, idx int\n   432→\t)\n   433→\tfor r, cnt := range req.Reason {\n   434→\t\tif idx == 0 {\n   435→\t\t\treason0, reason0Cnt = r, cnt\n   436→\t\t} else if idx == 1 {\n   437→\t\t\treason1, reason1Cnt = r, cnt\n   438→\t\t} else {\n   439→\t\t\tbreak\n   440→\t\t}\n   441→\t\tidx++\n   442→\t}\n   443→\n   444→\tswitch len(req.Reason) {\n   445→\tcase 0:\n   446→\t\treturn \"unknown\"\n   447→\tcase 1:\n   448→\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%s:%d\", reason0, reason0Cnt)\n   449→\tcase 2:\n   450→\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%s:%d and %s:%d\", reason0, reason0Cnt, reason1, reason1Cnt)\n   451→\tdefault:\n   452→\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%s:%d and %d(%d) more reasons\", reason0, reason0Cnt, len(req.Reason)-1,\n   453→\t\t\treq.Reason.Count()-reason0Cnt)\n   454→\t}\n   455→}\n   456→\n   457→func doSendPushes(stopCh <-chan struct{}, semaphore chan struct{}, queue *PushQueue) {\n   458→\tfor {\n   459→\t\tselect {\n   460→\t\tcase <-stopCh:\n   461→\t\t\treturn\n   462→\t\tdefault:\n   463→\t\t\t// We can send to it until it is full, then it will block until a pushes finishes and reads from it.\n   464→\t\t\t// This limits the number of pushes that can happen concurrently\n   465→\t\t\tsemaphore <- struct{}{}\n   466→\n   467→\t\t\t// Get the next proxy to push. This will block if there are no updates required.\n   468→\t\t\tclient, push, shuttingdown := queue.Dequeue()\n   469→\t\t\tif shuttingdown {\n   470→\t\t\t\treturn\n   471→\t\t\t}\n   472→\t\t\trecordPushTriggers(push.Reason)\n   473→\t\t\t// Signals that a push is done by reading from the semaphore, allowing another send on it.\n   474→\t\t\tdoneFunc := func() {\n   475→\t\t\t\tqueue.MarkDone(client)\n   476→\t\t\t\t<-semaphore\n   477→\t\t\t}\n   478→\n   479→\t\t\tproxiesQueueTime.Record(time.Since(push.Start).Seconds())\n   480→\t\t\tvar closed <-chan struct{}\n   481→\t\t\tif client.deltaStream != nil {\n   482→\t\t\t\tclosed = client.deltaStream.Context().Done()\n   483→\t\t\t} else {\n   484→\t\t\t\tclosed = client.StreamDone()\n   485→\t\t\t}\n   486→\t\t\tgo func() {\n   487→\t\t\t\tpushEv := &Event{\n   488→\t\t\t\t\tpushRequest: push,\n   489→\t\t\t\t\tdone:        doneFunc,\n   490→\t\t\t\t}\n   491→\n   492→\t\t\t\tselect {\n   493→\t\t\t\tcase client.PushCh() <- pushEv:\n   494→\t\t\t\t\treturn\n   495→\t\t\t\tcase <-closed: // grpc stream was closed\n   496→\t\t\t\t\tdoneFunc()\n   497→\t\t\t\t\tlog.Infof(\"Client closed connection %v\", client.ID())\n   498→\t\t\t\t}\n   499→\t\t\t}()\n   500→\t\t}\n   501→\t}\n   502→}\n   503→\n   504→// initPushContext creates a global push context and stores it on the environment. Note: while this\n   505→// method is technically thread safe (there are no data races), it should not be called in parallel;\n   506→// if it is, then we may start two push context creations (say A, and B), but then write them in\n   507→// reverse order, leaving us with a final version of A, which may be incomplete.\n   508→func (s *DiscoveryServer) initPushContext(req *model.PushRequest, oldPushContext *model.PushContext, version string) *model.PushContext {\n   509→\tpush := model.NewPushContext()\n   510→\tpush.PushVersion = version\n   511→\tpush.JwtKeyResolver = s.JwtKeyResolver\n   512→\tpush.InitContext(s.Env, oldPushContext, req)\n   513→\n   514→\ts.dropCacheForRequest(req)\n   515→\ts.Env.SetPushContext(push)\n   516→\n   517→\treturn push\n   518→}\n   519→\n   520→func (s *DiscoveryServer) sendPushes(stopCh <-chan struct{}) {\n   521→\tdoSendPushes(stopCh, s.concurrentPushLimit, s.pushQueue)\n   522→}\n   523→\n   524→// Shutdown shuts down DiscoveryServer components.\n   525→func (s *DiscoveryServer) Shutdown() {\n   526→\ts.closeJwksResolver()\n   527→\ts.pushQueue.ShutDown()\n   528→}\n   529→\n   530→// Clients returns all currently connected clients. This method can be safely called concurrently,\n   531→// but care should be taken with the underlying objects (ie model.Proxy) to ensure proper locking.\n   532→// This method returns only fully initialized connections; for all connections, use AllClients\n   533→func (s *DiscoveryServer) Clients() []*Connection {\n   534→\ts.adsClientsMutex.RLock()\n   535→\tdefer s.adsClientsMutex.RUnlock()\n   536→\tclients := make([]*Connection, 0, len(s.adsClients))\n   537→\tfor _, con := range s.adsClients {\n   538→\t\tselect {\n   539→\t\tcase <-con.InitializedCh():\n   540→\t\tdefault:\n   541→\t\t\t// Initialization not complete, skip\n   542→\t\t\tcontinue\n   543→\t\t}\n   544→\t\tclients = append(clients, con)\n   545→\t}\n   546→\treturn clients\n   547→}\n   548→\n   549→// SortedClients returns all currently connected clients in an ordered manner.\n   550→// Sorting order priority is as follows: ClusterID, Namespace, ID.\n   551→func (s *DiscoveryServer) SortedClients() []*Connection {\n   552→\tclients := s.Clients()\n   553→\tsort.Slice(clients, func(i, j int) bool {\n   554→\t\tif clients[i].proxy.GetClusterID().String() < clients[j].proxy.GetClusterID().String() {\n   555→\t\t\treturn true\n   556→\t\t}\n   557→\t\tif clients[i].proxy.GetNamespace() < clients[j].proxy.GetNamespace() {\n   558→\t\t\treturn true\n   559→\t\t}\n   560→\t\treturn clients[i].proxy.GetID() < clients[j].proxy.GetID()\n   561→\t})\n   562→\treturn clients\n   563→}\n   564→\n   565→// AllClients returns all connected clients, per Clients, but additionally includes uninitialized connections\n   566→// Warning: callers must take care not to rely on the con.proxy field being set\n   567→func (s *DiscoveryServer) AllClients() []*Connection {\n   568→\ts.adsClientsMutex.RLock()\n   569→\tdefer s.adsClientsMutex.RUnlock()\n   570→\treturn maps.Values(s.adsClients)\n   571→}\n   572→\n   573→func (s *DiscoveryServer) WaitForRequestLimit(ctx context.Context) error {\n   574→\tif s.RequestRateLimit.Limit() == 0 {\n   575→\t\t// Allow opt out when rate limiting is set to 0qps\n   576→\t\treturn nil\n   577→\t}\n   578→\t// Give a bit of time for queue to clear out, but if not fail fast. Client will connect to another\n   579→\t// instance in best case, or retry with backoff.\n   580→\twait, cancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, time.Second)\n   581→\tdefer cancel()\n   582→\treturn s.RequestRateLimit.Wait(wait)\n   583→}\n   584→\n   585→func (s *DiscoveryServer) NextVersion() string {\n   586→\treturn time.Now().Format(time.RFC3339) + \"/\" + strconv.FormatUint(s.pushVersion.Inc(), 10)\n   587→}\n   588→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. If updates are debounce they will be merged.\n\tvar req *model.PushRequest\n\n\tfree := true\n\tfreeCh := make(chan struct{}, 1)\n\n\tpush := func(req *model.PushRequest, debouncedEvents int, startDebounce time.Time) {\n\t\tpushFn(req)\n\t\tupdateSent.Add(int64(debouncedEvents))\n\t\tdebounceTime.Record(time.Since(startDebounce).Seconds())\n\t\tfreeCh <- struct{}{}\n\t}\n\n\tpushWorker := func() {\n\t\teventDelay := time.Since(startDebounce)\n\t\tquietTime := time.Since(lastConfigUpdateTime)\n\t\t// it has been too long or quiet enough\n\t\tif eventDelay >= opts.debounceMax || req.Full)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tfree = false\n\t\t\t\tgo push(req, debouncedEvents, startDebounce)\n\t\t\t\treq = nil\n\t\t\t\tdebouncedEvents = 0\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\ttimeChan = req.Merge(r)\n\t\tcase <-timeChan:\n\t\t\tif free {\n\t\t\t\tpushWorker()\n\t\t\t}\n\t\tcase <-stopCh:\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc configsUpdated(req *model.PushRequest) string {\n\tconfigs := \"\"\n\tfor key := range req.ConfigsUpdated {\n\t\tconfigs += key.String()\n\t\tbreak\n\t}\n\tif len(req.ConfigsUpdated) > 1 {\n\t\tmore := \" and \" + strconv.Itoa(len(req.ConfigsUpdated)-1) + \" more configs\"\n\t\tconfigs += more\n\t}\n\treturn configs\n}\n\nfunc reasonsUpdated(req *model.PushRequest) string {\n\tvar (\n\t\treason0, reason1            model.TriggerReason\n\t\treason0Cnt, reason1Cnt, idx int\n\t)\n\tfor r, cnt := range req.Reason {\n\t\tif idx == 0 {\n\t\t\treason0, reason0Cnt = r, cnt\n\t\t} else if idx == 1 {\n\t\t\treason1, reason1Cnt = r, cnt\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t\tidx++\n\t}\n\n\tswitch len(req.Reason) {\n\tcase 0:\n\t\treturn \"unknown\"\n\tcase 1:\n\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%s:%d\", reason0, reason0Cnt)\n\tcase 2:\n\t\treturn len(req.Reason)-1,\n\t\t\treq.Reason.Count()-reason0Cnt)\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc doSendPushes(stopCh <-chan struct{}, semaphore chan struct{}, queue *PushQueue) {\n\tfor {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-stopCh:\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t// We can send to it until it is full, then it will block until a pushes finishes and reads from it.\n\t\t\t// This limits the number of pushes that can
